<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">We have well established processes to allow interested parties to contact us through our Office of the Ombudsman. Our Office of the Ombudsman can be contacted by email to directors@te.com, through the Internet at </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">http://www.te.com/usa-en/about-te/corporate-responsibility/governance/ombudsman.html#chapter-4-dl</font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;"> or through mail at TE Connectivity, Office of the Ombudsman, 1050 Westlakes Drive, Berwyn, Pennsylvania 19312.
